## THE HIGH KINGDOM OF HARADWAITH ###						
#####################################						
#####################################

### In order:
## Haruzan
# House of Ayerikkä, Kings of Haruzan
# House of Aharuz, Ancient Kings of Haruzan before last alliance
# House of Amrûnomä, Gondor-supported old kings of Haruzan
# House of Ikendakä
# House of Prochalomin
# House of Kussikä
# House of Tacfimin
# House of Kamal, Castamiri Lords of Anacalimon
# Khäz-Gramaze Heads of Faith

## Haruze Borderlords
# House of Awzalikä, Lords of Amonost
# House of Qûtaibin, Lords of Haraegardh
# House of Salomonin, Lords of Dirnen
# House of Yahyakä, Lords of Carnen
# House of Sallakä, Lords of Imladrim

## Chelkar
# House of Khadnom, Lords of Chelkar
# House of Medjanom, Claimants of the Pezarsan throne

## Pezarsan
# House of Arzagarnom, Kings of Pezarsan
# House of Pesikkä, Ancient Kings of Pezarsan
# Brutish Southern Tribesmen

## Haradrim Lords of Umbar
# House of Adîrjan

## Jelut rulers near Umbar
# House of Zhajomin
# House of Tirsakounikä
# House of Mêlênkoud
# House of Izrissas
